***чувство.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чувство.html>чу́вство</a> (420)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čuvьstvo</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čuti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sense, feel, notice</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ьstvo</i>. Cognate to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чуять.html>чу́ять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čújatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чутье.html>чутьё</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čutʹjó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чувство.html>чу́вство</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čúvstvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чувство.html>чу́вства</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чувство.html>чу́вства</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чувство.html>чу́вств</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sense, feeling (sensation)</li>
<li>feeling, emotion</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чувствовать.html>чу́вствовать</a> (302)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чувствуемый.html>чу́вствуемый</a> (302)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чувствуемый.html>чу́вствуемый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čúvstvujemyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present passive imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чувствовать.html>чу́вствовать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čúvstvovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***чугун.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугу́н</a> (13261)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> borrowing. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chuvash_language" class="extiw" title="w:Chuvash language">Chuvash</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="cv"><a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугу́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čugun</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt">чуен</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">çuyen</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугу́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čugún</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугуна́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугуны́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугуно́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cast iron
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:серый.html>се́рый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугу́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">séryj <b>čugún</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">gray cast iron</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бе́лый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугу́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bélyj <b>čugún</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">white cast iron</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">переде́льный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугу́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">peredélʹnyj <b>čugún</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">pig iron</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">чу́шковый <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугу́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čúškovyj <b>čugún</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">pig iron</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">ко́вкий <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугу́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kóvkij <b>čugún</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">malleable iron</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>cooking pot <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">traditionally made of cast iron</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чугунок.html>чугуно́к</a> (18560)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чугун.html>чугу́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čugún</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чудесный.html>чуде́сно</a> (12553)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чудесный.html>чуде́сный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čudésnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чудесный.html>чуде́сно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čudésno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>miraculously, by a miracle</li>
<li>wonderfully, wonderful
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́ти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цветок.html>цветы́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чудесный.html>чуде́сно</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пахнуть.html>пахнут</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éti cvetý <b>čudésno</b> paxnut</i> ― <span class="e-translation">these flowers smell wonderful</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чудесный.html>чуде́сно</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:выглядеть.html>вы́глядишь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ty <b>čudésno</b> výgljadišʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you look wonderful</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li>it is wonderful
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здесь.html>здесь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чудесный.html>чуде́сно</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zdesʹ <b>čudésno</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">it is wonderful here</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чудо.html>чудеса́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čudesá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чудесный.html>чуде́сный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čudésnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>wonderful, miraculous
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чудесный.html>чуде́сное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:избавление.html>избавле́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čudésnoje</b> izbavlénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">miraculous escape</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>wonderful, lovely, beautiful, marvellous
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чудесный.html>чуде́сный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó <b>čudésnyj</b> vid</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he looks wonderful/splendid</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***чудиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чудиться.html>чу́диться</a> (7911)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čuditi</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чудиться.html>чу́диться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čúditʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почудиться.html>почу́диться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to seem <i>(to)</i>, to appear <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чудиться.html>чу́дится</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>čúditsja</b>, što</i> ― <span class="e-translation">it seems to him that; he seems to see (hear) that; he imagines that</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чудиться.html>чу́дится</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стук.html>стук</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>čúditsja</b> stuk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he seems to hear (it seems to him that he hears) a knock</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казаться.html>каза́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kazátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:видеться.html>ви́деться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vídetʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слышаться.html>слы́шаться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">slýšatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***чудо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чудо.html>чу́до</a> (1023)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čudo</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чудо.html>чу́до</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čúdo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чудо.html>чу́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чудо.html>чудеса́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чудо.html>чуде́с</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>miracle, marvel</li>
<li>wonder
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:семь.html>семь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чудо.html>чуде́с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́та</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">semʹ čudés svéta</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Seven Wonders of the World</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чудовище.html>чудо́вище</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čudóvišče</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чудо.html>чу́до</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čúdo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:действие.html>де́йствие</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">déjstvije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-енный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чудодейственный.html>чудоде́йственный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čudodéjstvennyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)чудоде́йственнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)чудоде́йственней</b>)

<ol><li>miraculous</li>
<li>amazing, extraordinary</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чужой.html>чужо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čužój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-би́на</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-bína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. For the suffix, compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ложбина.html>ложби́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ložbína</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hollow, depression, shallow ravine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***чуждый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чуждый.html>чу́ждый</a> (5135)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">щоуждь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">štuždĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ťuďь</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чужой.html>чужо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čužój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чуждый.html>чу́ждый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čúždyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чуждый.html>чу́ждый</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>foreign, strange, alien <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ dative or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dlja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + genitive, to someone/something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> foreign to, not possessing, deprived of, without <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ genitive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чуждый.html>чу́ждый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:самолюбие.html>самолю́бия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čúždyj</b> samoljúbija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">without self-esteem</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***чужеземец.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чужеземец.html>чужезе́мец</a> (16604)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чужой.html>чужо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čužój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>земля́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zemljá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ец</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чужеземец.html>чужезе́мец</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čužezémec</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чужеземец.html>чужезе́мца</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чужеземец.html>чужезе́мцы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чужеземец.html>чужезе́мцев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>stranger, foreigner (person in a foreign land)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чужой.html>чужо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čužój</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">foreign</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-e-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rod</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">origin, kind</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чужеродный.html>чужеро́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čužeródnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)чужеро́днее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)чужеро́дней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> alien, foreign, strange</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> alien to the body, rejected by the body</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***чужой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чужой.html>чужо́й</a> (5343)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ťuďь</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чуждый.html>чу́ждый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čúždyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чужой.html>чужо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čužój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>someone else’s, another’s, other’s</li>
<li>alien, strange, foreign</li>
<li>alien, stranger, foreigner, outsider</li></ol>

***чулок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чулок.html>чуло́к</a> (6467)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">чулъкъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čulŭkŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чулок.html>чуло́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čulók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чулок.html>чулка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чулок.html>чулки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:чулок.html>чуло́к</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>stocking
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can we date this quote?)</span>,  Leo Tolstoy,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/ru:%D0%90%D0%BD%D0%BD%D0%B0_%D0%9A%D0%B0%D1%80%D0%B5%D0%BD%D0%B8%D0%BD%D0%B0_(%D0%A2%D0%BE%D0%BB%D1%81%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B9)/%D0%A7%D0%B0%D1%81%D1%82%D1%8C_I/%D0%93%D0%BB%D0%B0%D0%B2%D0%B0_XXII" class="extiw" title="s:ru:Анна Каренина (Толстой)/Часть I/Глава XXII">Anna Karenina</a></cite>, <a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Anna_Karenina/Part_One/Chapter_22" class="extiw" title="s:Anna Karenina/Part One/Chapter 22">part I, chapter 22</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повернуть.html>поверну́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крутой.html>кру́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свою́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дама.html>да́му</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:открыться.html>откры́лись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тонкий.html>то́нкие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ножка.html>но́жки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ажурный.html>ажу́рных</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чулок.html>чулка́х</a></b></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">povernúl krúto svojú dámu, tak što otkrýlisʹ jejó tónkije nóžki v ažúrnyx <b>čulkáx</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">he turned his partner sharply round, so that her slim ankles, in light transparent stockings, were exposed to view</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
